 The nationwide agitation against the citizenship law is being seen by linking CAA with NRC and the people's anger against the Citizenship Amendment Act (CAA) is not being named

 Under the Citizenship Amendment Act, there is a provision for granting citizenship of the country to non-muslim refugees who came to India from Pakistan, Bengal and Afghanistan
 CAA main sirf hindu-jain-sikh-isai-parsi-baudhdhashrnarthiyon ko naagarikta mil sakegi

 "why are questions arising on NRC? Muslim organizations and leaders claim that CAA is just the first phase to implement NRC across the country
" agar NRC puure desh main aata he, to jin logon ko bahari bataaya jayega usamen adhiktar sankhya muslim samudaay kii ho sakati he
 The argument is also that if people from any other community come out of the NRC, then they can be given citizenship through the new law, but the Muslim community will have a direct impact
 assam main jari he viroxm main hui NRC main iskaa udhaaharan dikhaa tha, jisamen muslim samudaay ke logon se zyada gaiyr-muslim kii sankhya zyada thi

 isiilie naagarikta sanshodhan bill ke khilaaf assam ke log sadakon par pradarshan lagaataar badhata ja rahaa he

 During the rainy season it is very important to take care of wooden furniture
 visheshgyon kaa kahana he ki furniture ke konon, uske nichle or pichley bhaagon ko maheene main kam se kam ek baar jarur saaf karnaa chahie, khaskar monsoon ke dauraan yah jarur karen
 Vipul Amar and Harsheen Arora, founders of The Wee Renaissance, Deepak Asar, visual merchandising manager at Rentomajo, have made these suggestions regarding furniture care
 safar main janaa he? aise karen gahanon kii packing1
 Keep your wooden furniture away from doors, windows, so that it does not come in contact with rain water or leakage
 2
 The polish of the furniture also makes it strong, shiny and durable, so always apply a coat of lacquer (rogan) or varnish in two years, so that the knuckles or small holes will fill and it will last longer
 3
 Lacquer spray can be easily used for small furniture, which is available at the nearest hardware store
 4
 Put the washer under the leg to prevent the furniture leg from being exposed to floor moisture
 kapadon ko banaae rakhana he nayaa, apanaaen ye 6 tips5
 Keep the house clean, which will ensure the right level of humidity in the house, which is compatible with wooden furniture

 6
 lakdi ke furniture ko saaf karne ke liye geele kapade kaa istemaal nahin karen, balki saaf, sookhe kapade kaa istemaal karen
 7
 monsoon ke dauraan lakdi kaa furniture nami ke chalate phool jaataa he, isse dror kholane or band karne main dikkat hoti he
